msg:I rarely write reviews, but this Oriental Wenting in Lishui is really the hotel with the worst service during this Chinese New Year trip, no doubt about it! The appearance of the hotel looks pretty good among local hotels. After all, it is an old hotel, and we can't compare the facilities with new hotels, but the service is really something that makes me who stayed during the Chinese New Year unable to help but write a review. First, we drove to the hotel by ourselves, opened the trunk and asked the doorman to help us unload the luggage, but he ignored me directlyğŸ™„ Then, I, a girl, moved three boxes to the door, and the person at the door was indifferent... This is looking for trouble during the Chinese New Year... Then, after successfully getting the room, there was a pile of paid drinks neatly on the TV counter when I entered the door. I called and said that I needed to send two more bottles of water. The waiter told me that except for the two small bottles of poor Kuangquan water on the sink, everything else needs to be charged... It's the Chinese New Year, it's not that I can't afford your two bottles of water, but the difference from the courtesy I received in other hotels before is a bit too big. Not to mention that Kuangquan water is free, even the drinks and alcohol in the refrigerator are free. Drinking or not is one thing, and I feel that the respect I receive is too far away! Come, post pictures to feel it. ps: After I complained to the front desk manager, he reluctantly gave me another three bottles of water the next day... In short, there is no Chinese New Year service, everything costs money, those who are not short of money can do as they please, and those who mind can reasonably avoid the pit...

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Classic 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:1
posted:Posted January 26, 2024
msg:Entering the hotel, none of the waiters you meet will greet you. The first thing you see when you enter the room is a row of paid drinks under the TV and on the bar, and two bottles of small-capacity mineral water are given for free. At that time, I was thinking that this hotel was probably quite stingy. As expected, the child at home called the service desk to send two bottles of water, and then called the grandparents in the next room to order two bottles of water. As a result, the service desk actually said, "Why did you order water again?" A five-star hotel would treat a child like this, is it right? The hotel breakfast waiters all had iron faces, as if the guests owed them, and there was no spirit of active service. Is this the corporate culture of the hotel? The coffee delivered was cold. When asked if they had cappuccino, they said, "Isn't latte the same?" If not, then no, but are latte and cappuccino the same? The quality of toilet paper in the bathroom is very poor. I stayed in several hotels during this Lishui tour, and this hotel is not a little worse than Jinyun Jinjiang International Hotel. Also, although the Dongyang Guantianyuan Holiday Villa in Songyang County is not a five-star hotel, the hotel staff was very caring and attentive from the time we entered the hotel to the time we left, which made us feel very warm.
